et s’il ne puet revenir ensi, si fai gesir lou malaide sor son dos sus terre, et fiche .i. passeil fermement en terre entre ses cuixes, et lie drapelz entor, qu’il ne blece lou malaide;	If it cannot return to its place, if you make the patient lie on his back on the ground, and stretch his legs firmly in the earth between his thighs, and place a cloth around his waist, that he does not bleed the patient;
puis teigne li ministres la cuixe, et uns autres ministres estende lou piet a ses mains ou a .i. liien, k’il lie sus le col dou piet;	Then hold the arm firmly, and another assistant should extend the limb at his hands or wrists, which is placed on the collar of the limb;
puis estende chescuns ministres igalment, et li passelz soit adés entre les cuixes dou malaide por retenir le malaide quant on l’estent;	Then extend the thumbs of both assistants equally, and hold the patient’s body either between the thighs or below the armpits to hold the patient when extending it;
puis mette li mires igal la dislocation a ses mains, et uns autres ministres teigne la jambe sainne au desoz, et li dislocation revenra hastanment.	Then he sets the dislocation with his hands, and another attendant grasps the limb firmly at the shoulder, and the dislocation returns immediately.
Et quant elle iert a point, si met l’emplastre et estoupes sus, et l’estrain forment, et lie lou piet a la jambe, et warde les ners qui sont sus la cheville derrier, que li liiens ne soit trop estrois;	When it returns to its place, he puts on the dressing and binds tightly, and the strain is formed, and he grasps the limb at the ankle, and keeps the nerves above the heel from being too tight;
puis le laisse .ij. jors ou .iij., et se li liiens amolist, si l’estrain; puis le deslie au tier jor ou au quart, et deffent a aler lou malaide par .iiij. jors;	Then he leaves it for one or two days, and if the strain has subsided, he unbinds it a third or a fourth time, and the patient is allowed to walk again after three days.
et s’il va devant cel termine, ce n’est mie seurtez qu’il ne desalue encor.	And if he goes before this time, it is not certain that he will not suffer further pain.
Et se apostemes chaus i vient, si covient que tu l’apaises, si com nos avons dit autre part, tant qu’il soit sanez.	If the shoulder dislocates again after being reset, as we have mentioned elsewhere, then you must hold it still until it is healed.
des dois	If the shoulder dislocates again after being reset, as we have mentioned elsewhere, then you must hold it still until it is healed.
Quant li doi sont desaluez, si les covient bellement estendre sens travail, et c’est legiere chose.	When the head of the shoulder is dislocated due to moisture, and it is reset but cannot stay in place, repeatedly dislocating with slight movement as we have experienced, then you must first reset the dislocation.
Et se li dislocations est en aucun nout dou dos dou piet, si covient que tu faices seoir le malaide sus .i. leu plain ou sus .ie. table tot droit, et met ton piet sus ce qui apert de ces jointures, puis presse a ton piet forment, tant qu’il reviegne;	If the shoulder is dislocated from the socket, if you must hold the patient sitting upright on a chair or table, and put your hand on the area around the dislocation, then press your hand firmly until it returns to its normal position.
et quant il est igalz, et il n’i apert nient, si met desoz la plante dou piet une table a .ij. chiés, puis l’estrain forment, et le laisse .iij. jors, puis le deslie; et le fai reposer, tant qu’il soit sanez.	And when they are even, and nothing appears to be open, if you put on the salve of rue marguerite a dose of three quarters of a pound, then the swelling will form, and leave it for two days, then take it off; and rest it until it is healed.
de plaie et de dislocation ensamble	And when they are even, and nothing appears to be open, if you put on the salve of rue marguerite a dose of three quarters of a pound, then the swelling will form, and leave it for two days, then take it off; and rest it until it is healed.
Quant plaie vient avec la dislocation, et on la vuet restorer, maintes fois avient que li malaides muert:	And when they are even, and nothing appears to be open, if you put on the salve of rue marguerite a dose of three quarters of a pound, then the swelling will form, and leave it for two days, then take it off; and rest it until it is healed.
si ne soies mie presumptuous en la cure, se tu n’es saiges en l’art et tu ne l’as useit longement, et se tu n’es pitous et misericors et tardis, ne mie hardis;	If you are not confident in your skill for the cure, and if you are not learned in the art and have not used it for a long time, and if you are not compassionate and merciful and prompt, do not attempt it;
et use au comencement de choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et laisse le malaide en la main Deu, se tu n’i vois esperance de santeit;	If you do not use calming things at the beginning and leave the patient in the hand of God, if you do not see hope of health;
et quant tu i vois esperance, si ramoinne maintenant le membre au leu, ainsois que li apostemes chaus i viegne;	and when you see hope, if you now reset the limb, so that the abscesses remain alive;
et quant li membres est a leu, si aministre choses apaisans aposteme chaut, et cure la plaie, si com il covient, d’oignemens desiccatis;	and when the limb is set, if you administer calming things at the base of the wound, and cure the wound, as it should be, with desiccated oil;
et se avec la dislocation a brisure, et os menus desevrez, si les oste, et fai ce que nos avons dit en maladies simples;	And if with the dislocation there is a fracture, and the smaller bones break, if the bones themselves, do as we have said in simple ailments.
et te garde d’entrer en voie de paour, selonc ce que j’ai dit, car ce te vaut mues selonc ton Creator, et por la saveteit de t’arme et de ton cors. Amen	And take care not to enter into a state of fear, as I have said, for this will bring you suffering according to your Creator, and for the salvation of your soul and your body. Amen.
Explicit le romen de fisique	Praise the works of physical healing.
